The `public contributions` by users in Austria on `2024/12/19 8:14 AM UTC`. This list contains users from `Austria` and cities `Vienna` `Salzburg` `Innsbruck` `Linz` `Graz` `Klagenfurt` `Bregenz` `Villach`.

There are `9 countries` and `68 cities` can be found [here](https://github.com/fdeniz07/top-github-users).

There are `947 users`  in Austria. You need at least `47 followers` to be on this list.

## üì¶ Third party

- [@octokit/graphql](https://www.npmjs.com/package/@octokit/graphql) - Send GraphQL requests to GitHub API.
- [fs-extra](https://www.npmjs.com/package/fs-extra) - Creating directories and files.
